Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 21, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/hero/wizardslogo_thumb.jpg)
By Meghan Wolff and Jacob Van Lunen











Modern weekend is sure to highlight some of the format's newest and most exciting decks. Players around the world are hungry for innovative deck lists that are ready to rise to new competitive heights in the wake of Eye of Ugin's banning. We'll have to wait until Sunday for our main course, but we've got an appetizer for you this Saturday morning.


Here in Charlotte there were a whopping twenty-three players that earned a pair of byes in this weekend's event by going undefeated in Grand Prix Trial tournaments. Joseph Ng won the sole Sealed Deck qualifier - the other twenty-two winners and their decks can be found below.







#### Brandon Lambs - Affinity


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
